end_date\\n),\\ntop_products_tier1 AS (\\n    SELECT \\n        t.sku_code,\\n        pm.class_name,\\n        SUM(t.price * t.quantity) AS net_sales\\n    FROM transaction t\\n    JOIN guest_tagging g ON t.customer_code = g.customer_code\\n    JOIN product_master pm ON t.sku_code = pm.sku_code\\n    CROSS JOIN latest_12_months l\\n    WHERE g.most_often_purchased_city_tier = 1\\n      AND t.paid_date >= l.start_date AND t.paid_date <= l.end_date\\n    GROUP BY t.sku_code, pm.class_name\\n    ORDER BY net_sales DESC\\n    LIMIT 10\\n),\\ntop_products_tier2 AS (\\n    SELECT \\n        t.sku_code,\\n        pm.class_name,\\n        SUM(t.price * t.quantity) AS net_sales\\n    FROM transaction t\\n    JOIN guest_tagging g ON t.customer_code = g.customer_code\\n    JOIN product_master pm ON t.sku_code = pm.sku_code\\n    CROSS JOIN latest_12_months l\\n    WHERE g.most_often_purchased_city_tier = 2\\n      AND t.paid_date >= l.start_date AND t.paid_date <= l.end_date\\n    GROUP BY t.sku_code, pm.class_name\\n    ORDER BY net_sales DESC\\n    LIMIT 10\\n)\\nSELECT \'Tier 1\' AS city_tier, sku_code, class_name, net_sales FROM top_products_tier1\\nUNION ALL\\nSELECT \'Tier 2\' AS
